<script>
  var result = {};
  var volumes = {};

  x.forEach((key, value) => {
      var string1 = "";
      key.Descriptors.forEach((keyD1, valueD1) => {
          if (keyD1.Type != "ID") return;
          string1 = keyD1.Name;
          volumes[string1] = {};
      });

      key.Children.forEach((keyC1, valueC1) => {
          if (keyC1.Name == "VOLUMES") {
            volumes[string1] = [];

            keyC1.Children.forEach((keyC2, valueC2) => {
              volumes[string1][valueC2] = {};

              keyC2.Descriptors.forEach((keyC3, valueC3) => {
                if (keyC3.Type == "ID") {
                  volumes[string1][valueC2].source = keyC3.Name;
                }
              });

              keyC2.Children.forEach((keyC3, valueC3) => {
                volumes[string1][valueC2].target = keyC3.Descriptors[0].Name;
              });
            });
          }
      });
  });

  x.forEach((key, value) => {
      var string1 = "";
      key.Descriptors.forEach((keyD1, valueD1) => {
          if (keyD1.Type != "ID") return;
          string1 = keyD1.Name;
          result[string1] = {};
      });

      key.Children.forEach((keyC1, valueC1) => {
          console.log(string1, keyC1.Name, keyC1.Children)
          if (keyC1.Name == "OBJECTIVES") {
            result[string1].objectives = [];

            keyC1.Children.forEach((keyC2, valueC2) => {
              result[string1].objectives[valueC2] = {};

              keyC2.Descriptors.forEach((keyC3, valueC3) => {
                if (keyC3.Type == "SPAWN_POSITION") {
                  result[string1].objectives[valueC2].spawn_position = keyC3.Coordinate;
                }

                if (keyC3.Type == "LINKED_VOLUME") {
                  volumes[string1].forEach((vol) => {
                    if (vol.source == keyC3.Name) {
                      result[string1].objectives[valueC2].linked_volume = vol.target;
                    }
                  });
                }

                if (keyC3.Type == "0xC20AF349") {
                  volumes[string1].forEach((vol) => {
                    if (vol.source == keyC3.Name) {
                      result[string1].objectives[valueC2].unknown_volume = vol.target;
                      result[string1].objectives[valueC2].unknown_volume_source = vol.source;
                    }
                  });
                }

                if (keyC3.Type == "CONFIG") {
                  result[string1].objectives[valueC2].config = keyC3.Name;
                }
              });

              keyC2.Children.forEach((keyC3, valueC3) => {
                if (keyC3.Name == "POTENTIAL_SPAWN_POSITIONS") {
                  result[string1].objectives[valueC2].potential_spawn_positions = [];
                  keyC3.Children.forEach((keyC4, valueC4) => {
                    result[string1].objectives[valueC2].potential_spawn_positions.push(keyC4.Descriptors[1].Coordinate);
                  });
                }
              });
            });
          }

          if (keyC1.Name == "VOLUMES") {
            keyC1.Children.forEach((keyC2, valueC2) => {
              keyC2.Descriptors.forEach((keyC3, valueC3) => {
                if (keyC3.Name == "VOL_LOCATION_REACHED") {
                  result[string1].location = keyC2.Children[0].Descriptors[0].Name;
                }
              });
            });
          }
      });
  });
  console.log(JSON.stringify(result, null, 4));
</script>
